 What is right and wrong for a child
 
 
 is baat kaa faisla maa-baap se behatar shaayad hi koi kar saktaa ho
 On the other hand, his mother and father are the first role models for almost every child
 parents kii choti se choti aadaten bhi bacchon par bahut gaharaa prabhaav daalati hai
 Imitation theory of psychology also proves that children learn social behavior from their parents
 vaise to parents kii ye bharsak koshish hoti he ki wo kuch bhi aisa na karen jiskaa bachche par galat asar ho lekin kai baar kuch aisi galtiyaan ho jaati hai or bachche unhen apane vyavhaar kaa hissaa bana lete hai
 In such a situation, these habits can prove to be harmful for them
 ye hai wo 7 baaten jinka har maa-baap ko khyaal rakhana chahie
 
 
 1
 kai baar ham apane luks or kariyar ko lekar khud kii aalochana karne lagate hai
 By doing this, you can do negative things about the beauty and success in the mind of the child
 jisaki vajah se aage chalakar use depressant or chidchidepan kii shikaayat ho sakati he
 2
 bahut se mata-pita ghanton phone par lage rahete hai
 Seeing them, their children also start demanding mobile at a very young age
 isse unki padhai par asar pad saktaa he
 3
 kai maa-baap kii yah aadat hoti he ki wo apane bacchon ko ladkaa yaa ladki hone ke anusaar vyavhaar karne ke liye kehete hai
 For example, if there is a girl, they are advised not to participate in sports and boys are advised to hide their feelings
 aisa karne se bacchon par nakaaratmak prabhaav padataa he
 4
 bacchon ke saamne kabhi bhi dhumrapaan na karen or na hi sharaab pien
 Doing this in front of children may make them feel that there is nothing wrong in smoking and drinking alcohol
 isse wo bahut kam umr main is gandi lat kaa shikaar ho sakate hai
 5
 apane bacchon kii tulana duusare bacchon se kabhi nahin kerani chahie
 Nor should you scold your children in front of other children for bringing down the number
 aisa karne se aapke bachche ke aatm-sammaan ko thes pahunch sakati he
 6
 agar aap apane bacchon ke saamne parivaar ke anya sadasyon ke saath ladate hai to iskaa un par bura asar pad saktaa he
 They may become very aggressive at this young age
 7
 Never hand over your children for small mistakes
 agar aap unhen choti- choti baton par sajaa dete hai to unamem virodh kii bhaavana ghar kar sakati he or ho saktaa he wo aapkaa sammaan karnaa bhi chhod den

 The story of the film 'lakshmi' is inspired by many true incidents, which are happening in this country indiscriminately
 'lakshmi' ek aaina he, samaaj kaa jahaan deh vyapaar ab bhi fal-phool rahaa he
 The story of the film revolves around a 14-year-old minor girl named Lakshmi, who lives in a small village in Hyderabad, whose father sold her to a woman for a few rupees
 us mahila ne munaafe ke liye use dalal ke haathon main saunp diya or phir lakshmi pahunch gai ek kothe par vahaan uske saath baar-baar balaatkaar hua, dheron julm hue magar vah ladki ek enjio kii sahaayta se sting oparation karwaakar unki kaid se nikalati he or pahunchati he adaalat tak

 kothe kii malkin ke role main shefali shah ne acha abhinay kiya he
 The film's director Nagesh Kukanoor is also cast in Dalal's role
 yah film nagesh kii style kii he, jisamen kahani kehane kaa tarika bada saral he
 The film was promoted by describing the battle of Lakshmi
 magar lakshmi kii ladaai kam or us par atyaachaar zyada dikhaaya gaya, jise ham kai baar parde par dekh chuke hai
 There is a lot of abusive language in the film and i think it is not necessary to use abusive language to make the film look real
 mujhe lagata he ki aisi filmon main agar itani gaaliyaan na hon to shaayad family audiyans bhi cinemagharon kaa rukh kar sakati he

 Entertainment value in the film is negligible, but there is a message that shocks the society
 mere khyaal se sirf masala filmein hi nahin balki aisi filmein bhi banani chahie, jo samaaj ko ek disha de

 According to Hindu religion, Lord Ganesha is worshiped before performing any auspicious work
 aisi manyata he ki bhagwaan ganesh kaa pujan karne se jivan kii sari pareshaaniyaan dur hoti hai

 Do not use Tulsi in the worship of Lord Ganesha2
 pujan menganapatiki aisi pratimaa prayog karen, jisamen sound baayen haath kii ore ghumi ho3
 Do not use the trunk of Ganpati with a trunk on the right hand side, it is believed that it is difficult to practice, Ganpati is happy late
 4
 Ganesha loves modak and musk
 isliye aisi murti kii puja karen jisamen modak or mooshak donon hon

 modak, fal kaa bhoga lagaaein
 Perform the Lord Ganesha Aarti

 a lunar eclipse occurs when the moon comes out of the Earth's shadow
 chandragrahan poornima ke din hi padataa hechandragrahan poornima ke din padataa he lekin har poornima ko chandra grahan nahin padataa he

 yah jhukaav takreeban 5 degree he isliye har baar chandramaa prithvi kii chaaya main pravesh nahin karata
 It escapes from the top or bottom
 yahi baat suryagrahan ke liye bhi sach he
 Solar eclipses are always on the new moon day because the size of the moon is about 4 times less than the size of the earth
 isaki chaaya prithvi par choti aakaar kii padati he isiilie purnataa kii sthiti main surya grahan prithvi ke ek chote se hisse se hi dekha ja saktaa he
